A min. in the chem. diffusion coeff. of lithium (DLi) was predicted by the model for strong attractive interactions between the intercalation species and the host matrix.  The DLi in the material was measured as a function of the lithium content by using the galvanostatic intermittent titrn. technique.  The diffusion coeff. was found 1.8×10-14 and 2.2×10-16 cm2 s-1 for LiFePO4 and FePO4, resp., with a min. in correspondence of the peak of the differential capacity.  The DLi has also been measured by AC impedance method for various lithium contents.  The calcd. values are in very good agreement with the previous calcd. ones.</div></div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref48"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref48" class="rightTabRefNumLink">48</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit48" data-doi="10.1016/j.electacta.2009.11.096"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Rui, X. H.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Ding, N.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Liu, J.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Li, C.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Chen, C. H.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Analysis of the chemical diffusion coefficient of lithium ions in Li<sub>3</sub>V<sub>2</sub>(PO<sub>4</sub>)<sub>3</sub> cathode material</span>. <i>Electrochim. Acta</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2010</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>55</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">2384</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">2390</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.electacta.2009.11.096</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit48R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">48</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Analysis of the chemical diffusion coefficient of lithium ions in Li3V2(PO4)3 cathode material</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Rui, X. H.; Ding, N.; Liu, J.; Li, C.; Chen, C. H.</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Electrochimica Acta</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2010</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">55</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">7</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">2384-2390</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">ELCAAV</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0013-4686</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier B.V.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">The chem. diffusion coeffs. of Li ions ( DLi+ ) in Li3V2(PO4)3 between 3.0 and 4.8 V are systematically detd. by cyclic voltammetry (CV), electrochem. impedance spectroscopy (EIS) and galvanostatic intermittent titrn. technique (GITT).  The DLi+ values are dependent on the voltage state of charge and discharge.  Based on the results from all the 3 techniques, the true diffusion coeffs. ( DLi+true) measured in single-phase region are at 10-9-10-10 cm2 s-1.  Its apparent diffusion coeffs. ( DLi+app) measured in 2-phase regions by CV and GITT range from 10-10 to 10-11 cm2 s-1 and 10-8 to 10-13 cm2 s-1, resp., depending on the potentials.  By the GITT, the DLi+ varies nonlinearly in a W shape with the charge-discharge voltage, which is ascribed to the strong interactions of Li+ with surrounding ions.  Finally, the chem. diffusion coeffs. of Li ions measured by CV, EIS and GITT are compared to each other.</div></div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref49"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref49" class="rightTabRefNumLink">49</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit49" data-doi="10.1039/c8ta08582j"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yu, Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Zhang, H.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yang, X.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Chen, Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Jia, Z.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yan, J.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Zhang, H.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Li, X.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Vapour induced phase inversion: preparing high performance self-standing sponge-like electrodes with a sulfur loading of over 10 mg cm<sup>–2</sup></span>. <i>J. Mater. Chem. A</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2018</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>6</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">24066</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">24070</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/c8ta08582j</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit49R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">49</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Vapour induced phase inversion: preparing high performance self-standing sponge-like electrodes with a sulfur loading of over 10 mg/cm2</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Yu, Ying; Zhang, Hongzhang; Yang, Xiaofei; Chen, Yuqing; Jia, Ziyang; Yan, Jingwang; Zhang, Huamin; Li, Xianfeng</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Materials Chemistry A: Materials for Energy and Sustainability</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2018</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">6</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">47</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">24066-24070</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JMCAET</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2050-7496</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">To obtain a satisfactory rate performance of lithium-sulfur (Li-S) batteries with a high sulfur loading, the vapor induced phase inversion (VIPI) process was used to prep. sponge-like porous electrodes.  It is suitable for various solvents, binders and materials on account of phase sepn. principles and produces electrodes with enhanced adhesive properties, high electrolyte uptake and improved capability in electron/ion transport.  As a result, batteries assembled with the VIPIE delivered a high initial discharge capacity of 1171 mA h/g and presented a capacity retention of 56.6% within 400 cycles at 0.5C.  Addnl., a high discharge capacity of 693 mA h/g could be also obtained at 2C due to the facilitated electron/ion transport.  An electrode with a high sulfur loading of 19 mg/cm2 could be realized.  The 10 mg/cm2 sulfur loaded VIPIE delivered a high capacity of 1300 mA h/g at 0.05C (equaling to an areal capacity of 13.0 mA h/cm2) and showed a high capacity retention of 90.7% within 60 cycles at 0.1C.</div></div></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i16">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge at <a href="/doi/10.1021/acsami.9b22746?goto=supporting-info" class="ext-link">https://pubs.acs.org/doi/10.1021/acsami.9b22746</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">Digital photos, characterization data, and electrochemical performance (<a href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.9b22746/suppl_file/am9b22746_si_001.pdf" class="ext-link">PDF</a>)</p></li></ul><p></p><div class="supInfoBoxOnFTP "><div class="sup-info-attachments"><ul><li><a class="suppl-anchor" href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.9b22746/suppl_file/am9b22746_si_001.pdf">am9b22746_si_001.pdf (1.41 MB)</a></li></ul></div></div><div id="rightTab-figshare-widget"></div><br><div class="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight" data-pb-dropzone="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight"><div data-widget-def="UX3HTMLWidget" data-widget-id="b84e6b6c-b4d0-4427-b286-3cf14d52d013" class="mb-4">

(function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	}); 

	$('.share_button').on('click', function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	$("#pane-m1con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Figures'});
	});

	});

	});

<script nonce="93188b656b0a075e-SJC">
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    const modalContainer = document.querySelector('.my-main-container');

    // Function to show the modal
    function showModal() {
        modalContainer.style.display = 'flex';
        document.querySelector('.overlay').style.display = 'block';
    }

    // Function to hide the modal when the close button is clicked
    function hideModal() {
        modalContainer.style.display = 'none';
        document.querySelector('.overlay').style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Hide the modal initially
    hideModal();

    // Function to handle clicks outside the modal
    function handleClickOutside(event) {
        // const modalContainer = document.querySelector(".my-main-container");
        // Check if the click target is not a child of the modal container
        if (!modalContainer.contains(event.target)) {
            hideModal();
        }
    }

    // Add a click event listener to the close button
    document
        .querySelector('.close-button')
        .addEventListener('click', hideModal);

    // Add a click event listener to the document to handle clicks outside the modal
    document.addEventListener('click', handleClickOutside);

    const screenHeight = window.innerHeight;
    function updateModalPosition() {
        const scrollY = window.scrollY;
        // console.log("scrollY= " + scrollY);
        // modalContainer.style.top = `${50 + scrollY}px`;
        modalContainer.style.top = `${scrollY + screenHeight / 2}px`;
        // console.log("new top= " + modalContainer.style.top);
    }

    // Update the modal position when the user scrolls
    window.addEventListener('scroll', updateModalPosition);

    // Initialize the modal position
    updateModalPosition();

    //---Cookie---
    // Function to set the cookie with a given name, value, and expiration time in days
    function setCookie(name, value, days) {
        var expires = '';
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
            expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();
            console.log(expires + 'this is expires dateUTC');
        }
        document.cookie = name + '=' + (value || '') + expires + '; path=/';
        // console.log("document.cookie is: " + document.cookie);
    }

    if (!document.cookie.includes('modalAd')) {
        // Show Modal
        showModal();

        // Set the cookie with the name "modalAd", value "true", and expiration of 3 day
        setCookie('modalAd', 'true', 3);
    } else {
        hideModal();
    }
});

</script>

<script nonce="93188b656b0a075e-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

        errormessage =
          "<p class='gdpr_err'><b>Please Enter a valid email address<b><p>";

      function init() {
        setTimeout(function () {
          var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
          if (cookieExist) {
            //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
            return false;
          } else {
            //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
            gdprMessage();
          }
          //Events
          $("#closebtn").on("click", hideForm);

          //Handle submit
          $("#gdpr-message-btn").on("click", function (event) {
            handleClick();
          });

          // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
          // $(document).click(function(event) {
          // 	event.stopPropagation();
          //   console.log(event.target);
          //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
          //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
          //     $(this).off();
          //   }
          // });
          $("#gdpr-con-btn").click(function () {
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            hideForm();
          });
        }, time);
      }

      //Show the message
      function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $("#gdpr-message-modal").show();
      }

      function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
          //Submit the form
          //Hide form
          if ($(".gdpr_err")) {
            $(".gdpr_err").hide();
          }

          $("#gdpr-message-content");
          //If successful then...
          setCookie("gdpr", "true");
          //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
          //Show error message
          gdprErrorMessage();
          //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
      }

      function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
          return false;
        } else {
          errorStatus = true;
          $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
      }

      function validateEmail(email) {
        var re =
          /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
      }

      function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
      }

      function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + "=([^;]+)"));
        if (match) return match[1];
      }

      function hideForm() {
        //And set cookie
        $("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag("event", "GDPR Modal", {
          event_category: "Pubs GDPR",
          event_label: "GDPR Dismissal",
        });
      }

      return {
        init: init,
      };
    })();

    $(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
  </script>
</p>
-->

                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="93188b656b0a075e-SJC">
var currentJournal = "ACS Applied Materials &amp;amp; Interfaces";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>
